{\n      \"repo\": \"mozilla/gecko-dev\",\n      \"path\": \"layout/base/OverflowChangedTracker.h\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Firefox CSS layout engine reflow pipeline is implemented across multiple C++ source files organized in the mozilla/gecko-dev repository's layout directory.\\n\\n## Frame Construction\\nThe frame construction subsystem is responsible for building the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in:\\n- layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h: Main frame constructor class that implements the BeginUpdate/EndUpdate lifecycle and frame tree building algorithms.\\n\\n## Block Layout Reflow\\nThe block layout reflow pipeline is the core of CSS layout for block-level elements:\\n- layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h: Reflow input parameters struct that contains all input to a reflow operation, including constrained width/height, margins, padding, and other state.\\n- layout/generic/ReflowOutput.cpp/h: Reflow output struct that frames use to return their computed size and other metrics back to their parents.\\n- layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h: State machine for block layout reflow, tracking line breaking and space management.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h: Implementation of block frame reflow, the most common frame type for CSS blocks.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h: Helper class for block reflow operations like sizing and placing block children.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockDebugFlags.h: Debug utilities for block layout.\\n\\n## Dirty-Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system marks frames that need reflow when style or content changes:\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h: Bit flags for frame state including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY and NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN which are the core dirty bits.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameState.cpp/h: Management of frame state bits.\\n- layout/base/nsFrameManager.cpp/h: Frame manager that tracks the frame tree and handles frame changes.\\n- layout/style/nsChangeHint.h: Change hint flags that indicate what layout/style updates are needed (reflow, repaint, etc.).\\n- layout/style/nsStyleChangeList.cpp/h: List of elements that have changed and their change hints.\\n- layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h: Manages style tree changes and propagates dirty bits through the frame tree.\\n- layout/painting/nsDisplayListInvalidation.cpp/h: Display list invalidation tracking when visual properties change.\\n\\n## Frame Base Classes\\nAll frame types inherit from base classes that define the reflow interface:\\n- layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp/h: The main nsIFrame base class defining Reflow(), DidReflow(), and other frame lifecycle methods.\\n- layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.cpp/h: Base class for frames that have children.\\n- layout/generic/nsLeafFrame.cpp/h: Base class for frames without children.\\n- layout/generic/nsAtomicContainerFrame.h: Atomic container frame for non-splittable containers.\\n\\n## Inline Layout\\nInline layout is handled separately and is critical for text and inline element layout:\\n- layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.cpp/h: Inline frame implementation.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h: Line layout engine for inline content.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h: Line box structure representing a line in inline layout.\\n\\n## Frame Depth-ordered list for efficient frame traversal.\\n\\n## Reflow Orchestration\\n- layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h: Presentation shell that orchestrates the reflow process, manages FrameNeedsReflow bits, and coordinates with the refresh driver.\\n- layout/base/nsPresContext.cpp/h: Presentation context managing document layout state.\\n- layout/base/nsRefreshDriver.cpp/h: Refresh driver that schedules and executes reflow.\\n\\n## Display List & Visual Invalidation\\n- layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp/h: Display list for painting and visual updates.\\n- layout.\\n- layout/generic/ViewportFrame.cpp/h: Root viewport frame.\\n- layout/generic/nsPageFrame.cpp/h and layout/generic/nsPageContentFrame.cpp/h: Page layout for print/pagination.\\n- layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsGridContainerFrame.cpp: CSS Grid layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsColumnSetFrame.cpp/h and layout/generic/ColumnSetWrapperFrame.cpp/h: Multi-column layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsPlaceholderFrame.cpp/h: Placeholder frames for positioned elements.\\n- layout/generic/nsSplittableFrame.cpp/h: Splittable frames for multi-page content.\\n- layout/generic/nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h: First-letter pseudo-element frames.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameSetFrame.cpp/h: HTML frameset layout.\\n\\n## Utilities & Helpers\\n- multiple C++ source files organized in the mozilla/gecko-dev repository's layout directory.\\n\\n## Frame Construction\\nThe frame construction subsystem is responsible for building the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in:\\n- layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h: Main frame constructor class that implements the BeginUpdate/EndUpdate lifecycle and frame tree building algorithms.\\n\\n## Block Layout Reflow\\nThe block layout reflow pipeline is the core of CSS layout for block-level elements:\\n- layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h: Reflow input parameters struct that contains all input to a reflow operation, including constrained width/height, margins, padding, and other state.\\n- layout/generic/ReflowOutput.cpp/h: Reflow output struct that frames use to return their computed size and other metrics back to their parents.\\n- layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h: State machine for block layout reflow, tracking line breaking and space management.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h: Implementation of block frame reflow, the most common frame type for CSS blocks.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h: Helper class for block reflow operations like sizing and placing block children.\\n- layout/generic/nsBlockDebugFlags.h: Debug utilities for block layout.\\n\\n## Dirty-Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system marks frames that need reflow when style or content changes:\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h: Bit flags for frame state including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY and NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN which are the core dirty bits.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameState.cpp/h: Management of frame state bits.\\n- layout/base/nsFrameManager.cpp/h: Frame manager that tracks the frame tree and handles frame changes.\\n- layout/style/nsChangeHint.h: Change hint flags that indicate what layout/style updates are needed (reflow, repaint, etc.).\\n- layout/style/nsStyleChangeList.cpp/h: List of elements that have changed and their change hints.\\n- layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h: Manages style tree changes and propagates dirty bits through the frame tree.\\n- layout/painting/nsDisplayListInvalidation.cpp/h: Display list invalidation tracking when visual properties change.\\n\\n## Frame Base Classes\\nAll frame types inherit from base classes that define the reflow interface:\\n- layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp/h: The main nsIFrame base class defining Reflow(), DidReflow(), and other frame lifecycle methods.\\n- layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.cpp/h: Base class for frames that have children.\\n- layout/generic/nsLeafFrame.cpp/h: Base class for frames without children.\\n- layout/generic/nsAtomicContainerFrame.h: Atomic container frame for non-splittable containers.\\n\\n## Inline Layout\\nInline layout is handled separately and is critical for text and inline element layout:\\n- layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.cpp/h: Inline frame implementation.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h: Line layout engine for inline content.\\n- layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h: Line box structure representing a line in inline layout.\\n\\n## Frame Tree Management\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameList.cpp/h: Doubly-linked list of frames.\\n- layout/base/FrameProperties.h: Property storage for frame objects.\\n- layout/base/DepthOrderedFrameList.cpp/h: Depth-ordered list for efficient frame traversal.\\n\\n## Reflow Orchestration\\n- layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h: Presentation shell that orchestrates the reflow process, manages FrameNeedsReflow bits, and coordinates with the refresh driver.\\n- layout/base/nsPresContext.cpp/h: Presentation context managing document layout state.\\n- layout/base/nsRefreshDriver.cpp/h: Refresh driver that schedules and executes reflow.\\n\\n## Display List & Visual Invalidation\\n- layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp/h: Display list for painting and visual updates.\\n- layout/painting/nsDisplayListInvalidation.cpp/h: Tracks display list changes for invalidation.\\n\\n## Special Layout Modules\\n- layout/generic/AbsoluteContainingBlock.cpp/h: Absolute positioning layout.\\n- layout/generic/ViewportFrame.cpp/h: Root viewport frame.\\n- layout/generic/nsPageFrame.cpp/h and layout/generic/nsPageContentFrame.cpp/h: Page layout for print/pagination.\\n- layout/generic/nsCanvasFrame.cpp: Root frame for HTML documents.\\n- layout/generic/ScrollContainerFrame.cpp/h: Scrollable container frames.\\n- layout/generic/nsFlexContainerFrame.cpp: Flexbox layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsGridContainerFrame.cpp: CSS Grid layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsColumnSetFrame.cpp/h and layout/generic/ColumnSetWrapperFrame.cpp/h: Multi-column layout.\\n- layout/generic/nsPlaceholderFrame.cpp/h: Placeholder frames for positioned elements.\\n- layout/generic/nsSplittableFrame.cpp/h: Splittable frames for multi-page content.\\n- layout/generic/nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h: First-letter pseudo-element frames.\\n- layout/generic/nsFrameSetFrame.cpp/h: HTML frameset layout.\\n\\n## Utilities & Helpers\\n- layout/base/nsIReflowCallback.h: Callback interface for post-reflow notifications.\\n- layout/base/nsAutoLayoutPhase.cpp/h: RAII helper for layout phase management.\\n- layout/base/OverflowChangedTracker.h: Tracks overflow changes that require reflow.\\n\\nTogether, these files implement the complete CSS layout engine pipeline: frame construction from the DOM, reflow
